@kvd322 –°–ª–∞–≤, –≤ —á–µ–º —Ç–æ—Ç –æ—à–∏–±–∫–∞ –º–æ–∂–µ—Ç –±—ã—Ç—å? –Ø –ø—Ä–æ—Å—Ç–æ –º–æ–∂–µ—Ç —Ä–µ–∞–ª—å–Ω–æ —á–µ—Ç–æ –Ω–µ –≤–∏–∂—É? –ù–µ —Ç–∞–∫ –ø–æ–Ω—è–ª —Å —ç—Ç–∏–º —Å—Ö–µ–º–∞–º–∏? –≠–≤–∞–ª—É–∞—Ç–æ—Ä –µ—Å–ª–∏ —á—Ç–æ —Ç—Ä—É, __init –ø—Ä–æ–∏—Å—Ö–æ–¥–∏—Ç, –Ω–æ –≤–æ—Ç initialize —É–∂–µ –Ω–µ —Å—Ä–∞–±–∞—Ç—ã–≤–∞–µ—Ç. –¢–æ –µ—Å—Ç—å —É—Å–ª–æ–≤–∏—è –Ω–µ –ø–æ–¥—Ö–¥–æ–¥—è—Ç –∏–ª–∏ –µ—â–µ —á—Ç–æ:
function add_to_binder(npc,ini,scheme,section,storage)
    init_storage(storage)
    log1("add_to_binder trade for npc "..tostring(npc:id()))
    local manager = npc:motivation_action_manager()

    -- evaluators 
    manager:add_evaluator(prop_trade_candidate, evaluator_trade_candidate("evaluator_trade_candidate", storage))
    manager:add_evaluator(prop_trade_response,  evaluator_trade_response("evaluator_trade_response", storage))
    manager:add_evaluator(evid_trade_execute,   property_evaluator_const(false))

    -- actions
    local action = {}

    action[actid_trade_request] = action_trade_request("act_trade_request", storage)
    action[actid_trade_negotiate] = action_trade_negotiate("act_trade_negotiate", storage)
    action[actid_trade_execute] = action_trade_execute("act_trade_execute", storage)
    action[actid_trade_cancel]  = action_trade_cancel("act_trade_cancel", storage)

    -- –î–æ–±–∞–≤–ª—è–µ–º –æ–±—â–∏–µ preconditions 
    if xr_motivator and xr_motivator.addCommonPrecondition then
        xr_motivator.addCommonPrecondition(action[actid_trade_request])
        xr_motivator.addCommonPrecondition(action[actid_trade_negotiate])
        xr_motivator.addCommonPrecondition(action[actid_trade_execute])
        xr_motivator.addCommonPrecondition(action[actid_trade_cancel])
    end

    -- –ü—Ä–∏–≤—è–∑–∫–∞ —Å–ø–µ—Ü–∏—Ñ–∏—á–Ω—ã—Ö preconditions/effects
    action[actid_trade_request]:add_precondition(world_property(prop_trade_candidate, true))
    action[actid_trade_request]:add_effect(world_property(prop_trade_candidate, false))
    manager:add_action(actid_trade_request, action[actid_trade_request])

    action[actid_trade_negotiate]:add_precondition(world_property(prop_trade_response, true))
    action[actid_trade_negotiate]:add_effect(world_property(prop_trade_response, false))
    manager:add_action(actid_trade_negotiate, action[actid_trade_negotiate])

    action[actid_trade_execute]:add_precondition(world_property(evid_trade_execute, true))
    action[actid_trade_execute]:add_effect(world_property(evid_trade_execute, false))
    manager:add_action(actid_trade_execute, action[actid_trade_execute])

    manager:add_action(actid_trade_cancel, action[actid_trade_cancel])
end

In reply to this message 
#include "game_graph.h"
struct CCC_JumpToLevel : public IConsole_Command
{
    CCC_JumpToLevel(LPCSTR N) : IConsole_Command(N){};

    virtual void Execute(LPCSTR args)
    {
        if (!ai().get_alife())
        {
            Msg("! ALife simulator is needed to perform specified command!");
            return;
        }
        string256 level;
        sscanf(args, "%s", level);

        GameGraph::LEVEL_MAP::const_iterator I = ai().game_graph().header().levels().begin();
        GameGraph::LEVEL_MAP::const_iterator E = ai().game_graph().header().levels().end();
        for (; I != E; ++I)
            if (!xr_strcmp((*I).second.name(), level))
            {
                ai().alife().jump_to_level(level);
                return;
            }
        Msg("! There is no level \"%s\" in the game graph!", level);
    }

    virtual void fill_tips(vecTips& tips, u32 mode)
    {
        if (!ai().get_alife())
        {
            Msg("! ALife simulator is needed to perform specified command!");
            return;
        }

        GameGraph::LEVEL_MAP::const_iterator itb = ai().game_graph().header().levels().begin();
        GameGraph::LEVEL_MAP::const_iterator ite = ai().game_graph().header().levels().end();
        for (; itb != ite; ++itb)
        {
            tips.push_back((*itb).second.name());
        }
    }
};

–∏–∑–Ω–∞—á–∞–ª—å–Ω–æ
local get_trade = function(way_name, props)
  if not props then
    local ptr = patrol(way_name)
    props = utils.parse_waypoint_data(way_name, ptr:flags(0), ptr:name(0))
  end
  
  if props.trade ~= nil then
      log3("Way point [%s] props:", gname)
      
    for k,v in pairs(props) do
      -- v = _G.type(v) ~= 'userdata' and tostring(v) or 'userdata'  -- —Ä–∞—Å–∫–æ–º–º–µ–Ω—Ç–∏—Ç—å, –µ—Å–ª–∏ –±—É–¥–µ—Ç –≤—ã–ª–µ—Ç
      log3("  %s = %s", k, v)
    end  
    
    local ltx_path = props.trade=="true" and "misc\\"..gname.."_trade" or props.trade
      log3("[%s] path to trade: '%s'", way_name, ltx_path)
    return "trade = "..ltx_path..".ltx\n"
  end
  
  return ""
end
